\DoxyCodeLine{566 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_STRING\_SIZE\_TYPE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{567 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_STRING\_SIZE\_TYPE unsigned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{568 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{569 }
\DoxyCodeLine{570     \textcolor{comment}{// A 24 byte string class (can be as small as 17 for x64 and 13 for x86) that can hold strings with length}}
\DoxyCodeLine{571     \textcolor{comment}{// of up to 23 chars on the stack before going on the heap -\/ the last byte of the buffer is used for:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{572     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ "{}is small"{} bit -\/ the highest bit -\/ if "{}0"{} then it is small -\/ otherwise its "{}1"{} (128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{573     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ capacity left before going on the heap -\/ using the lowest 5 bits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{574     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ 2 bits are left unused -\/ the second and third highest ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{575     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ if small -\/ acts as a null terminator if strlen() is 23 (24 including the null terminator)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{576     \textcolor{comment}{//              and the "{}is small"{} bit remains "{}0"{} ("{}as well as the capacity left"{}) so its OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{577     \textcolor{comment}{// Idea taken from this lecture about the string implementation of facebook/folly -\/ fbstring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{578     \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=kPR8h4-\/qZdk}}
\DoxyCodeLine{579     \textcolor{comment}{// TODO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{580     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ optimizations -\/ like not deleting memory unnecessarily in operator= and etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{581     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ resize/reserve/clear}}
\DoxyCodeLine{582     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ replace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{583     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ back/front}}
\DoxyCodeLine{584     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ iterator stuff}}
\DoxyCodeLine{585     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ find \& friends}}
\DoxyCodeLine{586     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ push\_back/pop\_back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{587     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ assign/insert/erase}}
\DoxyCodeLine{588     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ relational operators as free functions -\/ taking const char* as one of the params}}
\DoxyCodeLine{589     \textcolor{keyword}{class }DOCTEST\_INTERFACE \mbox{\hyperlink{classdoctest_1_1_string}{String}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3420 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3421         \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3422         \textcolor{keyword}{using }Atomic = T;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3423 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3424         \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3425         \textcolor{keyword}{using }Atomic = std::atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3426 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3427 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3428 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS) || defined(DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTITHREADING)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3429         \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3430         \textcolor{keyword}{using }MultiLaneAtomic = Atomic<T>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3431 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3432         \textcolor{comment}{// Provides a multilane implementation of an atomic variable that supports add, sub, load,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433         \textcolor{comment}{// store. Instead of using a single atomic variable, this splits up into multiple ones,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434         \textcolor{comment}{// each sitting on a separate cache line. The goal is to provide a speedup when most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3435         \textcolor{comment}{// operations are modifying. It achieves this with two properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437         \textcolor{comment}{// * Multiple atomics are used, so chance of congestion from the same atomic is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438         \textcolor{comment}{// * Each atomic sits on a separate cache line, so false sharing is reduced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440         \textcolor{comment}{// The disadvantage is that there is a small overhead due to the use of TLS, and load/store}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441         \textcolor{comment}{// is slower because all atomics have to be accessed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442         \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443         \textcolor{keyword}{class }MultiLaneAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3445             \textcolor{keyword}{struct }CacheLineAlignedAtomic}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3447                 Atomic<T> atomic\{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3448                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} padding[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_CACHE\_LINE\_SIZE -\/ \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(Atomic<T>)];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3449             \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3450             CacheLineAlignedAtomic m\_atomics[DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3451 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3490 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3491         \textcolor{keyword}{private}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492             \textcolor{comment}{// Each thread has a different atomic that it operates on. If more than NumLanes threads}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493             \textcolor{comment}{// use this, some will use the same atomic. So performance will degrade a bit, but still}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494             \textcolor{comment}{// everything will work.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495             \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496             \textcolor{comment}{// The logic here is a bit tricky. The call should be as fast as possible, so that there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497             \textcolor{comment}{// is minimal to no overhead in determining the correct atomic for the current thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498             \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499             \textcolor{comment}{// 1. A global static counter laneCounter counts continuously up.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500             \textcolor{comment}{// 2. Each successive thread will use modulo operation of that counter so it gets an atomic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501             \textcolor{comment}{//    assigned in a round-\/robin fashion.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502             \textcolor{comment}{// 3. This tlsLaneIdx is stored in the thread local data, so it is directly available with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503             \textcolor{comment}{//    little overhead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504             Atomic<T>\& myAtomic() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505                 \textcolor{keyword}{static} Atomic<size\_t> laneCounter;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506                 DOCTEST\_THREAD\_LOCAL \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} tlsLaneIdx =}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507                     laneCounter++ \% DOCTEST\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS\_THREAD\_LANES;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3509                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} m\_atomics[tlsLaneIdx].atomic;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511         \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif }\textcolor{comment}{// DOCTEST\_CONFIG\_NO\_MULTI\_LANE\_ATOMICS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4122     \textcolor{keyword}{namespace }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4123         \textcolor{keyword}{using namespace }detail;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4124         \textcolor{comment}{// matching of a string against a wildcard mask (case sensitivity configurable) taken from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4125         \textcolor{comment}{// https://www.codeproject.com/Articles/1088/Wildcard-\/string-\/compare-\/globbing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4126         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} wildcmp(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* wild, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} caseSensitive) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4127             \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* cp = str;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4128             \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4129 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4130             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} ((*str) \&\& (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4131                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((caseSensitive ? (*wild != *str) : (tolower(*wild) != tolower(*str))) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{4132                     (*wild != \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4133                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4134                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4135                 wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4136                 str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4137             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4138 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4139             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (*str) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4140                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4141                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!*++wild) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4142                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4143                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4144                     mp = wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4145                     cp = str + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4146                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4147                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((caseSensitive ? (*wild == *str) : (tolower(*wild) == tolower(*str))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4148                     (*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'?'})) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4149                     wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4150                     str++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4151                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4152                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4153                     wild = mp;   }
\DoxyCodeLine{4154                     str = cp++; }
\DoxyCodeLine{4155                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4156             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4157 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4158             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (*wild == \textcolor{charliteral}{'*'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4159                 wild++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4160             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4161             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} !*wild;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4162         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4163 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4563         \textcolor{comment}{// Returns true if the current process is being debugged (either}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4564         \textcolor{comment}{// running under the debugger or has a debugger attached post facto).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4565         \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} isDebuggerActive() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4566             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}        mib[4];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4567             kinfo\_proc info;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4568             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}     size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4569             \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize the flags so that, if sysctl fails for some bizarre}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4570             \textcolor{comment}{// reason, we get a predictable result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4571             info.kp\_proc.p\_flag = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4572             \textcolor{comment}{// Initialize mib, which tells sysctl the info we want, in this case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4573             \textcolor{comment}{// we're looking for information about a specific process ID.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4574             mib[0] = CTL\_KERN;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4575             mib[1] = KERN\_PROC;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4576             mib[2] = KERN\_PROC\_PID;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4577             mib[3] = getpid();}

\DoxyCodeLine{4702             FatalConditionHandler() \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4703                 isSet = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4704                 \textcolor{comment}{// 32k seems enough for doctest to handle stack overflow,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4705                 \textcolor{comment}{// but the value was found experimentally, so there is no strong guarantee}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4706                 guaranteeSize = 32 * 1024;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4707                 \textcolor{comment}{// Register an unhandled exception filter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4708                 previousTop = SetUnhandledExceptionFilter(handleException);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4709                 \textcolor{comment}{// Pass in guarantee size to be filled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4710                 SetThreadStackGuarantee(\&guaranteeSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4711 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4712                 \textcolor{comment}{// On Windows uncaught exceptions from another thread, exceptions from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4713                 \textcolor{comment}{// destructors, or calls to std::terminate are not a SEH exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4714 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4715                 \textcolor{comment}{// The terminal handler gets called when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4716                 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4717                 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM THE TEST RUNNER THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4718                 original\_terminate\_handler = std::get\_terminate();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4719                 std::set\_terminate([]() DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4720                     reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Terminate handler called"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4721                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (isDebuggerActive() \&\& !g\_cs-\/>no\_breaks)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4722                         DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4723                     std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE); \textcolor{comment}{// explicitly exit -\/ otherwise the SIGABRT handler may be called as well}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4724                     \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4725 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4726                 \textcolor{comment}{// SIGABRT is raised when:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4727                 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ std::terminate is called FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4728                 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an exception is thrown from a destructor FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4729                 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ an uncaught exception is thrown FROM A DIFFERENT THREAD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4730                 prev\_sigabrt\_handler = std::signal(SIGABRT, [](\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} signal) DOCTEST\_NOEXCEPT\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4731                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (signal == SIGABRT) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4732                         reportFatal(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}SIGABRT -\/ Abort (abnormal termination) signal"{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{4734                             DOCTEST\_BREAK\_INTO\_DEBUGGER();}
\DoxyCodeLine{4735                         std::exit(EXIT\_FAILURE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4736                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4737                     \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4738 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4739                 \textcolor{comment}{// The following settings are taken from google test, and more}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4740                 \textcolor{comment}{// specifically from UnitTest::Run() inside of gtest.cc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4741 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4742                 \textcolor{comment}{// the user does not want to see pop-\/up dialogs about crashes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4743                 prev\_error\_mode\_1 = SetErrorMode(SEM\_FAILCRITICALERRORS | SEM\_NOALIGNMENTFAULTEXCEPT |}
\DoxyCodeLine{4744                     SEM\_NOGPFAULTERRORBOX | SEM\_NOOPENFILEERRORBOX);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4745                 \textcolor{comment}{// This forces the abort message to go to stderr in all circumstances.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4746                 prev\_error\_mode\_2 = \_set\_error\_mode(\_OUT\_TO\_STDERR);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4747                 \textcolor{comment}{// In the debug version, Visual Studio pops up a separate dialog}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4748                 \textcolor{comment}{// offering a choice to debug the aborted program -\/ we want to disable that.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4749                 prev\_abort\_behavior = \_set\_abort\_behavior(0x0, \_WRITE\_ABORT\_MSG | \_CALL\_REPORTFAULT);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4750                 \textcolor{comment}{// In debug mode, the Windows CRT can crash with an assertion over invalid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4751                 \textcolor{comment}{// input (e.g. passing an invalid file descriptor). The default handling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4752                 \textcolor{comment}{// for these assertions is to pop up a dialog and wait for user input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4753                 \textcolor{comment}{// Instead ask the CRT to dump such assertions to stderr non-\/interactively.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5163             \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} trailingBytes(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5164                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xE0) == 0xC0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5165                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5166                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5167                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF0) == 0xE0) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{5169                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5170                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((c \& 0xF8) == 0xF0) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5171                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5172                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5173                 DOCTEST\_INTERNAL\_ERROR(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}Invalid multibyte utf-\/8 start byte encountered"{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{5178                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} c \& 0x1F;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5179                 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{5189             \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} hexEscapeChar(\mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& os, \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5190                 std::ios\_base::fmtflags f(os.flags());}
\DoxyCodeLine{5191                 os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)x"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5192                     << std::uppercase << std::hex << std::setfill(\textcolor{charliteral}{'0'}) << std::setw(2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5193                     << \textcolor{keyword}{static\_cast<}\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\textcolor{keyword}{>}(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5194                 os.flags(f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5195             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5196 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5197         \} \textcolor{comment}{// anonymous namespace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5198 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5199         XmlEncode::XmlEncode(std::string \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& str, ForWhat forWhat)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5200             : m\_str(str),}
\DoxyCodeLine{5201             m\_forWhat(forWhat)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5202         \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5203 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5204         \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} XmlEncode::encodeTo(\mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& os)\textcolor{keyword}{ const }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5205             \textcolor{comment}{// Apostrophe escaping not necessary if we always use "{} to write attributes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5206             \textcolor{comment}{// (see: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5207 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5208             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t idx = 0; idx < m\_str.size(); ++idx) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5209                 uchar c = m\_str[idx];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5210                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (c) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5211                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'<'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&lt;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5212                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\&'}:   os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&amp;"{}}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5213 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5214                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'>'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5215                     \textcolor{comment}{// See: https://www.w3.org/TR/xml/\#syntax}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5216                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx > 2 \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 1] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'} \&\& m\_str[idx -\/ 2] == \textcolor{charliteral}{']'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{5217                         os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&gt;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5218                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5219                         os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5220                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5221 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5222                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)"{}'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5223                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (m\_forWhat == ForAttributes)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5224                         os << \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\&quot;"{}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5225                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5226                         os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5227                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5228 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5229                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{5230                     \textcolor{comment}{// Check for control characters and invalid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5231 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5232                     \textcolor{comment}{// Escape control characters in standard ascii}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5233                     \textcolor{comment}{// see https://stackoverflow.com/questions/404107/why-\/are-\/control-\/characters-\/illegal-\/in-\/xml-\/1-\/0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5234                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x09 || (c > 0x0D \&\& c < 0x20) || c == 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5235                         hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5236                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5237                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5238 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5239                     \textcolor{comment}{// Plain ASCII: Write it to stream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5240                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0x7F) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5241                         os << c;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5242                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5243                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5244 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5245                     \textcolor{comment}{// UTF-\/8 territory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5246                     \textcolor{comment}{// Check if the encoding is valid and if it is not, hex escape bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5247                     \textcolor{comment}{// Important: We do not check the exact decoded values for validity, only the encoding format}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5248                     \textcolor{comment}{// First check that this bytes is a valid lead byte:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5249                     \textcolor{comment}{// This means that it is not encoded as 1111 1XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5250                     \textcolor{comment}{// Or as 10XX XXXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5251                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c < 0xC0 ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5252                         c >= 0xF8) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5253                         hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5254                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5255                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5256 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5257                     \textcolor{keyword}{auto} encBytes = trailingBytes(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5258                     \textcolor{comment}{// Are there enough bytes left to avoid accessing out-\/of-\/bounds memory?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5259                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (idx + encBytes -\/ 1 >= m\_str.size()) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5260                         hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5261                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5262                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5263                     \textcolor{comment}{// The header is valid, check data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5264                     \textcolor{comment}{// The next encBytes bytes must together be a valid utf-\/8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5265                     \textcolor{comment}{// This means: bitpattern 10XX XXXX and the extracted value is sane (ish)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5266                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} valid = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5267                     uint32\_t value = headerValue(c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5268                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 1; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5269                         uchar nc = m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5270                         valid \&= ((nc \& 0xC0) == 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5271                         value = (value << 6) | (nc \& 0x3F);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5272                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5273 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5274                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (}
\DoxyCodeLine{5275                         \textcolor{comment}{// Wrong bit pattern of following bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5276                         (!valid) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5277                         \textcolor{comment}{// Overlong encodings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5278                         (value < 0x80) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5279                         (value < 0x800 \&\& encBytes > 2) || \textcolor{comment}{// removed "{}0x80 <= value \&\&"{} because redundant}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5280                         (0x800 < value \&\& value < 0x10000 \&\& encBytes > 3) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{5281                         \textcolor{comment}{// Encoded value out of range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5282                         (value >= 0x110000)}
\DoxyCodeLine{5283                         ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5284                         hexEscapeChar(os, c);}
\DoxyCodeLine{5285                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5286                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5287 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5288                     \textcolor{comment}{// If we got here, this is in fact a valid(ish) utf-\/8 sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5289                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (std::size\_t n = 0; n < encBytes; ++n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5290                         os << m\_str[idx + n];}
\DoxyCodeLine{5291                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5292                     idx += encBytes -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{5293                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{5294                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5295             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5296         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5297 }
\DoxyCodeLine{5298         \mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& operator << (\mbox{\hyperlink{classstd_1_1basic__ostream}{std::ostream}}\& os, XmlEncode \textcolor{keyword}{const}\& xmlEncode) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{5299             xmlEncode.encodeTo(os);}

\DoxyCodeLine{6493         \textcolor{comment}{// the implementation of parseOption()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6494         \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} parseOptionImpl(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} argc, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* \textcolor{keyword}{const}* argv, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* pattern, String* value) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6495             \textcolor{comment}{// going from the end to the beginning and stopping on the first occurrence from the end}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6496             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = argc; i > 0; -\/-\/i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6497                 \textcolor{keyword}{auto} index = i -\/ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{6498                 \textcolor{keyword}{auto} temp = std::strstr(argv[index], pattern);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6499                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (temp \&\& (value || strlen(temp) == strlen(pattern))) \{ }
\DoxyCodeLine{6500                     \textcolor{comment}{// eliminate matches in which the chars before the option are not '-\/'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6501                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} noBadCharsFound = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6502                     \textcolor{keyword}{auto} curr = argv[index];}
\DoxyCodeLine{6503                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (curr != temp) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6504                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (*curr++ != \textcolor{charliteral}{'-\/'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6505                             noBadCharsFound = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6506                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{6507                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6508                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6509                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (noBadCharsFound \&\& argv[index][0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'-\/'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6510                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (value) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6511                             \textcolor{comment}{// parsing the value of an option}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6512                             temp += strlen(pattern);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6513                             \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} len = strlen(temp);}
\DoxyCodeLine{6514                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{6515                                 *value = temp;}
